data-v-content="true"><h2 data-v="" id="cast-nonce">cast nonce<a aria-label="Link to this section" class="heading-anchor" href="/reference/cast/nonce#cast-nonce" data-v-link="true" data-v="true"><svg <p data-v="">Get the nonce for an account</p>
<div data-v-terminal-container="true" class="vocs:flex vocs:flex-col"><div data-v-terminal-item="true" data-v-terminal-type="command" class="vocs:[&amp;_[data-v-code-container]]:my-0 vocs:[&amp;_[data-v-code-container]]:rounded-b-none vocs:[&amp;_[data-v-code-container]]:border-b-0 vocs:[&amp;_[data-v-code-container]_pre]:rounded-b-none data-v-shell="" data-v="true"><code data-language="bash" data-v="true"><span class="line" data-v-shell-line=""><span style="color:light-dark(#6F42C1, #F69D50);--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#F69D50" data-v-shell-prompt="">$ </span><span style="color:light-dark(#032F62, #96D0FF);--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#96D0FF">cast</span><span style="color:light-dark(#032F62, #96D0FF);--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#96D0FF"> nonce</span><span style="color:light-dark(#005CC5, #6CB6FF);--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#6CB6FF"> --help</span></span></code><button aria-label="Copy code" class="vocs:absolute vocs:top-2.5 vocs:data-[single-line=true]:top-1/2 vocs:data-[single-line=true]:-translate-y-1/2 vocs:right-2.5 vocs:p-1.5 vocs:data-[copied=true]:opacity-100 vocs:data-[copied=true]:text-success" data-copied="false" data-single-line="false" type="button"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1em" height="1em" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="vocs:size-4"><g fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" vocs:[&amp;_[data-v-code-container]]:rounded-t-none vocs:[&amp;_[data-v-code-container]_pre]:rounded-t-none"><div data-v-code-container="true"><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark-dimmed vocs:relative vocs:group/code" tabindex="0" data-v="true"><code data-language="txt" data-v="true"><span class="line"><span>Usage: cast nonce [OPTIONS] &lt;WHO&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>Arguments:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  &lt;WHO&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          The address to get the nonce for</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>Options:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  -B, --block &lt;BLOCK&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          The block height to query at.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          </span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          Can also be the tags earliest, finalized, safe, latest, or pending.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  -h, --help</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          Print help (see a summary with &#x27;-h&#x27;)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  -j, --threads &lt;THREADS&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          Number of threads to use. Specifying 0 defaults to the number of</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          logical cores</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          </span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          [aliases: --jobs]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>Rpc options:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  -r, --rpc-url &lt;URL&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          The RPC endpoint, default value is http://localhost:8545</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          </span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          [env: ETH_RPC_URL=]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  -k, --insecure</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          Allow insecure RPC connections (accept invalid HTTPS certificates).</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          </span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          When the provider&#x27;s inner runtime transport variant is HTTP, this</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          configures the reqwest client to accept invalid certificates.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>      --no-proxy</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          Disable automatic proxy detection.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          </span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          Use this in sandboxed environments (e.g., Cursor IDE sandbox, macOS</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          App Sandbox) where system proxy detection causes crashes. When</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          enabled, HTTP_PROXY/HTTPS_PROXY environment variables and system proxy</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          settings will be ignored.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>      --flashbots</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          Use the Flashbots RPC URL with fast mode</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          ([https://rpc.flashbots.net/fast](https://rpc.flashbots.net/fast)).</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          </span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          This shares the transaction privately with all registered builders.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          </span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          See:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          [https://docs.flashbots.net/flashbots-protect/quick-start#faster-transactions](https://docs.flashbots.net/flashbots-protect/quick-start#faster-transactions)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>      --jwt-secret &lt;JWT_SECRET&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          JWT Secret for the RPC endpoint.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          </span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          The JWT secret will be used to create a JWT for a RPC. For example,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          the following can be used to simulate a CL `engine_forkchoiceUpdated`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          call:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          </span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          cast rpc --jwt-secret &lt;JWT_SECRET&gt; engine_forkchoiceUpdatedV2</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          &#x27;[&quot;0x6bb38c26db65749ab6e472080a3d20a2f35776494e72016d1e339593f21c59bc&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          &quot;0x6bb38c26db65749ab6e472080a3d20a2f35776494e72016d1e339593f21c59bc&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          &quot;0x6bb38c26db65749ab6e472080a3d20a2f35776494e72016d1e339593f21c59bc&quot;]&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          </span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          [env: ETH_RPC_JWT_SECRET=]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>      --rpc-timeout &lt;RPC_TIMEOUT&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          Timeout for the RPC request in seconds.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          </span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          The specified timeout will be used to override the default timeout for</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          RPC requests.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          </span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          Default value: 45</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          </span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          [env: ETH_RPC_TIMEOUT=]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>      --rpc-headers &lt;RPC_HEADERS&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          Specify custom headers for RPC requests</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          </span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          [env: ETH_RPC_HEADERS=]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>      --curl</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          Print the equivalent curl command instead of making the RPC request</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>Display options:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>      --color &lt;COLOR&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          The color of the log messages</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          Possible values:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          - auto:   Intelligently guess whether to use color output (default)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          - always: Force color output</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          - never:  Force disable color output</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>      --json</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          Format log messages as JSON</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>      --md</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          Format log messages as Markdown</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  -q, --quiet</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          Do not print log messages</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  -v, --verbosity...</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          Verbosity level of the log messages.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          </span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          Pass multiple times to increase the verbosity (e.g. -v, -vv, -vvv).</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          </span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          Depending on the context the verbosity levels have different meanings.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          </span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          For example, the verbosity levels of the EVM are:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          - 2 (-vv): Print logs for all tests.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          - 3 (-vvv): Print execution traces for failing tests.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          - 4 (-vvvv): Print execution traces for all tests, and setup traces</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          for failing tests.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          - 5 (-vvvvv): Print execution and setup traces for all tests,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>          including storage changes and</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>            backtraces with line numbers.</span></span></code><button aria-label="Copy code" class="vocs:absolute vocs:top-2.5 vocs:data-[single-line=true]:top-1/2 vocs:cursor-pointer vocs:group-hover/code:opacity-100 vocs:data-[copied=true]:opacity-100 vocs:data-[copied=true]:text-success" data-copied="false" data-single-line="false" type="button"><svg \"}]}]\n6c:[\"$\",\"span\",null,{\"className\":\"line\",\"children\":[\"$\",\"span\",null,{\"children\":\"          For example, the verbosity levels of the EVM
